If the file was renamed (e.g., `openclaw.mjs` → `evox.mjs`), this caused MODULE_NOT_FOUND crashes.\\n\\n## Root Cause\\n\\n1. Config change triggers gateway restart via SIGUSR1\\n2. If supervisor (launchd) detection fails, respawn falls back to spawning with `process.argv.slice(1)`\\n3. `process.argv[1]` contains the OLD filename from when process was originally started\\n4. If that file no longer exists → MODULE_NOT_FOUND → all agents crash\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nResolve entry point in order:\\n1. `OPENCLAW_ENTRY_POINT` env var (explicit override)\\n2. `package.json` bin field (current script name)\\n3. `process.argv[1]` (legacy fallback with debug log)\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\n- Added test: env override wins over stale argv\\n- Added test: package.json bin is used before
